< text>
I chose this company, because the ease of someone coming to you when your car won't start seemed like a no brainer. I was very impressed that I could get next day service in Portland, OR.

First appointment: I scheduled the appointment for Sunday afternoon (2:30 PM - 4:30) and spent two hours waiting. After two hours went by, I called to check the status and learned the technician cancelled the appointment. The company simply deflected by saying that there was an attempt to e-mail me and that I must not have received it, which was not true. The soonest availability was Tuesday Morning. I e-mailed the company to notify them of my disappointment on the initial interaction and did not receive a response.
Second appointment: The technician was confident that all I needed was a new battery, but then determined that this was not the case and that I would need a new starter and mentioned that they had a 1 PM available the next day (Wednesday) and that they would get that time reserved for me.
Third appointment: One hour went by on Wednesday and they told me they put in a contingency time for 4:00 PM - 6:00 PM in case the technician is delayed.
Fourth appointment: The technician couldn't make this later time happen. I was rescheduled for the following morning (Thursday) from 8:30 AM - 10:30 AM.
Fifth appointment: The company notified me by 8:10 AM that the technician was not going to make it and wanted to reschedule for the following morning (Friday).
Sixth appointment: By 8:30 AM, my appointment has already been pushed back to 10:30 AM to 12:30 PM. I made a note that this appointment has already been rescheduled numerous times and was offered $25 off.

Pros (this was not an entirely negative experience, which is why I am giving one star): online scheduling, text reminders, transparent pricing--I appreciate the fact that the price of the initial diagnostic will be reduced from my final repair price, in addition to the discount for so many reschedules. The technician was professional, kind, and understood my needs. I really enjoyed the interaction that I had with them and have been looking forward to having them work on my car again this week.

If I could do things over again, I would have just called my insurance company and had my car towed to the nearest shop. I would have preferred for my car to sit for a week in a shop instead of continuing to be disappointed on a daily basis thinking that my car was going to be looked at. I have been trying to get this vehicle fixed up so I can sell it and purchase a more family friendly vehicle and my experience with RepairSmith significantly reduced the expediency in which I was hoping to do that. What seems like convenience (online scheduling, text reminders, credit cards on file for contactless payment) made me think that it would be taken care of in a timely manner and was ultimately a big distraction for how disappointing the entire process was. I will never use this company again.<//text>

I'll be honest... I love this park. Very clean and children are always having fun here including my own babies. There is barbecue places, a field, and the location is right next to a school and down the street is a grocery store. 1574544351632</Date>
< Rate>
5</Rate>
< Review>
El Comal Family Restaurant is located in an old looking shopping center, the parking is terrible, and traffic in and out is atrocious.  However, once you open the door you enter a colorful tropical atmosphere, adorned with classic Hispanic artwork throughout. The food was good. I had the Caldo de Pollo (chicken soup) which was very good. The broth was light and well flavored, vegetables were cooked just right, and I was given a large piece of chicken (on the bone). The taste brought instant gratification, as it reminded me of the soup my grandmother would make when I was a child. We got a lot of food (see picture) for a great price. Everything pictured including drinks was just $27! If you are in the area, and not in a hurry, stop by and enjoy a bite to eat.< /Review>

< Review>
El Comal Family Restaurant is located in an old looking shopping center, the parking is terrible, and traffic in and out is atrocious.  However, once you open the door you enter a colorful tropical atmosphere, adorned with classic Hispanic artwork throughout. The food was good. I had the Caldo de Pollo (chicken soup) which was very good. The broth was light and well flavored, vegetables were cooked just right, and I was given a large piece of chicken (on the bone). The taste brought instant gratification, as it reminded me of the soup my grandmother would make when I was a child. We got a lot of food (see picture) for a great price. Everything pictured including drinks was just $27! If you are in the area, and not in a hurry, stop by and enjoy a bite to eat.< /Review>

< review>
My dad and mom were patrons of El Comal since the old location.  With mom gone now dad insists on his visits.  Hesitantly I always abided.  Customer Service is key for me.  Food is second.  Lets start with service.   And I understand not everyone is meant for the industry, but for the most part this staff is fine.  With the exception of one.  TAKE NOTE;  Ysenia far exceeds any exceptions one would find at a restaurant.  You typically find her level of service in fine dining.  i would definitely keep my eye on her and write my SOP (standard operating procedure) for all new hires that are going to be working the floor.

Now the food, as my dad is a fan, i became one too with reservation.  The food is good, all the dishes I've tried so far had been done well.  The pupusas are amazing if you eat there.  Don't take home.    Their Chile  Verde was also great.  Now thier hard shell shredded beef tacos are KILLER.  Why am i not raving about their food.  Well I am.  As i would of any other latin restaurant that served food my grandmother could easily out perform.  I am hispanic and know latin food.  I say this with love and in hopes my comments assist.  I could get this at most good mexican restaurants.  But who want good.  I want GREAT!  A little kick in authenticity would go a long way.  A pinch in presentation i believe essential.  I begin eating with my eyes before it touches my mouth.

We will be back, my father insists.  I love the new decor.  The bar looks amazing and $15 FOR BOTTOMLESS MIMOSA BRUCH!  Im there!!!  IF MY FATHER BELIEVES IN YOU IM SURE I WILL TOO!!!!!<//review>

< text>
El Comal is without a doubt this region's best choice for authentic Mexican style food. Place is beautiful. Should be a historical town landmark now that El Comal is occupying the spot. These guys were a hit decades before moving to this location. I'll eat at El Comal before I go to any of the other like cuisines here. I'm just happy they re-opened after their fire. Anyways take this advice... nowhere can you go in this town to find a better experience. They have a private party room for b-days, weddings, cinses, whatever. They have a bar with game television coverages that you can dine at as well as regular booth and table seating. Uber family friendly oriented. The decor is really cool. When the El Comal family had to move from their last place they used their insurance re-build money wisely. Their new location is bomb. Food is (as usual) bomb, people are no, not bomb... loveable and special. Good family operation. The Dogman of Lake Elsinore has spoken...so be it...and they all said...Amen!</text>
